SOGS PA GANG YIN PA SHES PAR 'GYUR RO, ,SNGON GYI GNAS SHES PAR
BYA BA NI ZHES PA TSE SNGA MA SHES PAR BYA BA NA SNYING PO GONG
DU SMOS PA RTAG TU BZLAS SHING SEMS RTZE GCIG TU BYAS NA SNGON
GANG NA GNAS PA TING NGE 'DZIN GYIS

RTOGS PAR GYUR TO, ,TSIG BSGRUB PAR 'DOD PAS ZHES PA BDAG GIS
TSIG JI SKAD SMRAS PA DE BZHIN DU 'GYUR RO, ,CHO 'PHRUL STON PA
NI ZHES PA RDO RJE H'Um KA RA'I SNYING PO RDO RJE TSIG GIS BZLAS
SO, ,SEMS CAN THAMS CAD PA'I GZUGS BRNYAN GYI TSUL DU STON TO
ZHES PA RANG GI LUS

NYID GZUGS GONG DU SMOS PA RNAMS KYI GZUGS BRNYAN DU SNANG NGO,
,RANG GI GZUGS CI DGA' BAR SGYUR BAR BYED CES PA H'Um KA RA'I
SNYING PO GONG DU SMOS LA RDO RJE'I TSIG SGRA MED CING SO DANG
MCHU BSDAMS LA LCE CUNG ZAD 'GUL BAS 'BUM BZLAS NA DE NAS NUB
GCIG MTSAN THAL

BZLAS PAS BSGRUB PO, MI SNANG BAR 'DOD PAS RDO RJE MI SNANG BA
PHRA MO RDO RJE KHU TSUR GYI CHANG PAR BCUG STE BZUNG LA DE NAS
MI SNANG BAR GYUR GYI BAR DU BZLAS SO, ,DE NAS CHANG PA NA RDO
RJE 'DUG PA BKROL TE BTANG NA SNANG BAR 'GYUR RO, ,KHRI LA 'DUG
NAS BLANGS TE ZHES PA SNGON

BSNYEN PA BYAS NAS SHING KHRI'U LA 'DUG STE MTSAN GCIG SGRUB PA'I
CHO GA BZHIN DU BSGRUB PO, KHRI'U NAM MKHA' LA 'PHAR NA GRUB PA
YIN TE DE LA ZHON NAS MTHO RIS MAN CHAD THAMS CAD DU 'GRO'O,
,GDON GYIS 'DZIN DU GZHUG NA ZHES BA 'BYUNG PO LA SOGS PA'I

@234A *, ,GDON GYIS DKON MCHOG GSUM LA NGAN DU BYED PA LA SOGS
PAR SBYAR RO, ,GDON GAR BYED DU GZHUG BA NI ZHES PA GDON MI LA
BABS PA GAR BYED DU GZHUG PA STE SNYING PO GONG DU SMOS PA'I 'JUG
TU HI ZHES BYA BAR BSKUL LO, ,GDON BSKYOD PA NI ZHES PA RMYA
ZHING NYAL BA DANG 'THEN PA

LTA BU LAS BSKUL ZHING BSKYOD PA'O, ,NOR DGUG PA NI RIN PO CHE
GTZO BO'I SEMS ZHES PA NOR MANG PO LA PHAL PO CHE 'DOD NA MAR GA
TA DANG PADMA R'A GAS SBYIN SREG GIS SHIG ,CHAR DBAB PA NI ZHES
PA RDO RJE H'Um KA RA'I RNAL 'BYOR BYAS LA SNYING PO GONG DU SMOS
PA STONG BZLAS SHING KLU THAMS CAD PHYOGS BZHI

NAS 'DUS TE CHAR 'BEBS BAR BSAM MO, CHAR GCAD BA NI ZHES PA GONG
MA BZHIN RNAL 'BYOR DU BYAS LA SNYING PO BZLAS TE CHAR DANG SPRIN
THAMS CAD RI RGYUD DAM TSIGS KYI PHA ROL TU PHYOGS TE BOR BAR BSAM
MO, SER BA GCAD PA NI ZHES PA RDO RJE H'Um KA RA'I RNAL 'BYOR
GONG MA BZHIN DU BYAS

LA SNYING PO YANG ZLOS SHING RDO RJE BCINGS PA'I PHYAG RGYAS
'DZAM BU'I GLING GI PHA ROL TU DOR BAR DMIGS TE PHYAG RGYA DGROL
LO, ,GDON DGAG PA'AM ZHES PA YANG GDON MI BSNYEN PA'O, ,SPRIN
DGAG PA NI ZHES BA SPRIN CHAR MI LTUNG BAR DGAG PA'O, ,BSAL BA

NI ZHES PA SPRIN BSAL TE SANGS PAR BYA'O, ,RDO RJE DKYIL 'KHOR
GYI STENG DU BZHAG NAS ZHES PA GSER DNGUL LAM ZANGS KYI RDO RJE
RTZE LNGA PA TZANDAN NAM LCI BA'I DKYIL 'KHOR BYAS PA'I STENG DU
BZHAG LA BSGRUB PO, NAM MKHA' LA ME TOG GI PHRENG BA CHAGS PAR
BYAS PA NI ZHES

PA BDAG RANG DBUGS SHIN TU BSDAMS LA RDO RJE KHU TSUR GYI PHYAG
RGYAS ME TOG NAM MKHA' LA GTOR TE RLUNG GI DKYIL 'KHOR GYIS BRTAN
PAR BSAM MO, CHA LUGS BZHAD PAR BYA NA ZHES PAS SANGS RGYAS DANG
BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' DANG 'JIG RTEN PA'I LHA LA SOGS PA'I

CHA LUGS GANG YANG RUNG BA'O, ,RDO RJE'I PHYAG RGYA NI PHYAG NA
RDO RJE'I PHYAG RGYA GONG DU SMOS PA SNYING GAR BZHAG STE SNGAGS
BZLAS SO, ,CHA LUGS DE NYID GAR BYED PA DANG SMRAR GZHUG PA DANG
BRGYUG PA DANG SMIN MA 'GUL BAR SBYAR RO, ,SA G-YO BAR BYAS NA
RKANG PA G-YON

@234B PA BRDAB PAS SO ZHES PA, RDO RJE H'Um KA RA'I RNAL 'BYOR DU
BYAS TE SNYING PO GONG DU SMOS PA ZLOS SHING RKANG PA G-YON PAS
SA LA DRAG TU BRDAB PO, KHYIM BSGUL BA NI ZHES PA KHYIM GYI 'KHOR
NYI TSE BSGUL BAR BYA NA 'KHOR RLUNG GIS RAB TU BSKYOD PAR BSAMS
TE PHYAG RGYA BCING NGO, ,RKANG

PA DGUG CES PA SEMS CAN GANG YANG RUNG KYO BA TANG GIS RKANG PA
NAS BZUNG STE DGUG PAR BYA'O, ,SPRIN MED PAR CHANG DBAB PA NI
ZHES PA NI NGO MTSAR BSTAN PAR BYA BA STE, RDO RJE H'Um KA RA'I
RNAL 'BYOR BYAS LA PHYOGS BZHI NAS SPRIN CHEN PO RLUNG GIS BSKYOD
CING KLU CHAR 'BAB

PAR BSAMS TE BZLAS SO, ,ZLA BA DANG NYI MA DBAB CING BSTAN PA NI
ZHES PA ZLA BA DANG NYI MA SA LA LTUNG BAR KUN LA BSTAN PA NI DE
BZHIN DU BSAMS LA RDO RJE SA LA BRDAB PO, NYI MA DANG ZLA BA MANG
PO BSTAN NA ZHES BA NAM MKHA' LA NYI ZLA MANG POS GANG BAR BSTAN
PA RDO RJE BZHI NAM MKHA'

LA GTOR RO, ,DMAG RNAM BZHI BSTAN NA ZHES PA GLU DANG GLANG PO
DANG RTA DANG RKANG THANG PA'I DMAG BZHI DGRA RNAMS KYIS MTHONG
BAR BSTAN PA'O, ,MTSAN MO NYIN PAR BYA NA RDO RJE RTZE LNGA PA
RAB TU 'BAR BAR BSAMS TE GLAD PA LA BSKOR RO, ,NYIN MO MTSAN MOR
BYA NA

SNGAGS PA NYID MIG BTZUMS LA THAMS CAD MUN PAR BSAMS TE RDO RJE
BSKOR RO, ,THAMS CAD LA RDO RJE BSTAN NA ZHES PA 'KHOR THAMS CAD

RTOG PA RDZOGS SO,, ,,DE NAS BCOM LDAN 'DAS DE BZHIN

GSHEGS PA DGRA BCOM PA YANG DAG PAR RDZOGS PA'I SANGS RGYAS KYIS

SEMS CAN GYI DON GYI PHYIR SNYING PO GSUNGS SO, ,DBANG BSKUR BAR

BZHIN TE THOB PAR BYA BA'I PHYIR NA DAM TSIG GO ZHES BYA BA DANG
SBYAR RO, ,YE SHES KYI RANG BZHIN DE SEMS CAN GYI DON SNA TSOGS
LA SNYING PO DANG PHYAG RGYA LA SOGS PA RNAM BA DU MAR

SBYOR BA YANG MI SLU BA'I PHYIR DE KHO NA ZHES BYA'O, ,SNYING PO
DANG PHYAG RGYA LA SOGS PA YANG BSDU NA LUS DANG NGAG DANG SEMS
RDO RJER 'DUS TE LUS KYI DKYIL 'KHOR DANG, NGAG GI DKYIL 'KHOR
DANG, SEMS KYI DKYIL 'KHOR DU SNYING PO LA SOGS PA THAMS CAD
GSUNGS PA'I PHYIR RO, ,DE LTAR LUS LA SOGS

PA RDO RJE THAMS CAD KYANG KHYOD KYIS SKYE BO MA LUS PA 'DUL BA'I
PHYIR SMRAS PA YIN TE, GDUL BA DE DAG GI DON GYI PHYIR DED KYI
BYIN GYIS BRLAB CES BYA BA'I DON TO, ,SGRUB PA PO RNAMS LA DE
BZHIN GSHEGS PAS BYIN GYIS BRLAB PAR BSKUL BA DANG, BYANG CHUB
KYI SEMS LA CHAGS PA MED KYANG SNGAGS 'DI BRJOD

NA 'GRUB PAR 'GYUR RO ZHES GSUNGS PA, DE BAS NA SGRUB PA PO DES
DANG POR ZHES PA DAG GO, ,DE NAS PHYAG NA RDO RJES RTOG PA 'DI'I
YON TAN BSNGAGS PA, SEMS CAN KUN LA PHAN PHYIR DU, ,ZHES BYA BA
DAG GO, ,MNYAM PA RU NI BSRUNGS NAS SO, ,ZHES PA SU 'DI LA NAN
TAN BYED PA THAMS CAD 'DAG

GIS MNYAM PAR SRUNG NGO ZHES PA'I DON TO, ,DE NAS BCOM LDAN 'DAS
RNAM PAR SNANG MDZAD KYI RDZU 'PHRUL BSTAN NAS PHYAG NA RDO RJE
LA LEGS PA BYIN PA, DE NAS BCOM LDAN 'DAS GDAN LAS BZHENGS TE
ZHES BYA BA DAG GO, ,KHAMS GSUM THAMS CAD LA SPRUL PA'I SKU PHRA
MOS GANG PAR BYAS ZHES BYA BA'I

DON TO, ,BLA MA MANG DU THOS PA'I MAN DAG LA, ,BRTEN TE MDO RU
'GREL PA 'DI BGYIS PAS, ,SKYE BO SGRIB PA'I MUN PAS KHEBS PA
RNAMS, ,SGRIB BYANG RDO RJE SEMS DPA'I THABS THOB SHOG ,'JIG RTEN
GSUM LAS RNAM PAR RGYAL BA'I 'GREL PA MU TI TA KO shAS BYAS PA
RDZOGS SO,, ,,
